 2006 kaa ye maamla em nagaraj kaa he

 How does the creamy layer of SC / ST differ from the creamy layer of OBC? The question arises that when the OBCK creamy layer does not get the benefit of reservation, then why should the creamy layer of SC-ST get the benefit of reservation? Ashok Kumar Bharti aajtak, President of the National Confederation of Dalit Organization
 in se baat karte hue kehete hai ki daliton or obisi ke krimi layer alag hote hai
 He says in support of his argument, "SC / ST have been socially, economically and historically disadvantaged, they were forced to stay out of society
 inke khilaaf anyaay kaa bhav ab bhi samaaj main barkaraar he
 This is not the case with obcs

 vah azamgarh ke alaava mainpuri loksabhaa seat se bhi chunaav lard rahe hai
 Around 1 in the afternoon
 30 baje mulaayam ne azamgarh colectrate main apana parchaa daakhil kiya
 He was accompanied by senior ministers of Uttar Pradesh government and local mlas of Azamgarh, Balram Yadav and Durga Prasad Yadav
 parchaa daakhil karne ke baad mulaayam ne colectrate se lekar itiai maidan tak road sho kiya
 Here he addressed a public meeting
 mulaayam ne bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke pradhanmantri pad ke ummidavaar narendra modi par hamalaa karte hue kaha ki pehle to bijepi kaa bahumat nahin aayega, agar ye sambhav bhi ho gaya to modi pradhanmantri nahin ban paaenge
 Modi hidden Rustomamoolayam said that there are so many 'hidden secrets' in BJP that they will not allow Modi to become Prime Minister
 dushkarm ke jurm main sajayaftaa yuvakon ke prati sahanubhuti rakhane vaale sapa pramukh ne phir doharaaya ki is chunaav main centre main tisare morche kii sarkaar kii banegi, jisamen sapa kii behad mahatvapurn bhoomika hogi
 Mulayam has promised in an election meeting that he will change the anti-rape law when he comes to power
 air india kii flite main staff ke saath marpet se charchaa main aae shivasena ke saansad rabindra gayakwad ne aaj us ghatana ko lekar loksabhaa main apana paksh rakhaa
 Ravindra complained of a media trial against him in Parliament and also apologized to the House, but the Shiv Sena's attitude over the matter has grown angry
 haalat ye he ki centre main mantri anant geete ne mumbai se koi flite na udne dene tak kii dhamkee de di he
 Meanwhile, Air India has sought additional security for its flights flying from Mumbai, Pune
 chappalmaar saansad kaa maafee se inkaarastr ke dauraan apane bhaashan main rabindra gayakwad ne air india se maafee maangane se saaf inkaar kiya lekin kaha ki yadi unhone koi durvyavhaar kiya he to ve sansad se maafee maangate hai
 After Ravindra, Anant Geete, MP from Shiv Sena and Minister of Heavy Industries and Public Entrepreneurship at the Center, also raised this issue and targeted Air India fiercely
 uddyan mantri rahe nishane parasadan kii kaarywahi jab sthagit hui to shivasena saansadon ne naagarik uddyan mantri ashok gajpati raju ko nishane par liya or raju hai-hai ke naare lagaae
 During this time, both sides got into trouble
 rajnath singh or smriti irani jaise duusare mantriyon ke bich-bachaav se yahaan apriy sthiti to tal gai lekin geete ne saaf dhamkee di ki agar ye maamla nahin sulajhaa to mumbai ko koi flite nahin udne di jaaegi
 Ravindra Gaikwad should ban ban: Athawale: Union Minister Ramdas Athawale says that what happened in the House should not have happened
 lekin shivasena saansadon kaa gussa tha
 The way his MP Ravindra Gaikwad is banned
 jahaaj main yatra karne ko lekar vah thik nahin he
 The ban should be lifted
 kanoon jo bhi he vah apni karrwai karegaa
 But it is not okay to stop someone from traveling
 sadan main jo hua durbhagyapurna: jayant sinhanagarik uddyan rajya mantri jayant sinha kaa kahana he ki jo sadan main hua he vah durbhagyapurna hona nahin chahie tha
 We are trying to find a way out
 kisi bhi vyakti ko jahaaj main yatra karnaa se rokna thik nahin: kalyaan banerjeetrunmul congress ke saansad kalyaan banerjee kaa kahana he kisi bhi saansad yah kisi bhi vyakti ko jahaaj main yatra karnaa se rokna yah uske moolbhoot adhikaron kaa hanan he
 It should not happen
 agar unka koi maamla he usamen kanoon apana kaam karegaa
 What was their behavior, no more
 usase hamako lenaa nahin he
 But the ban against them should be removed

 Karunanidhi grew up in the Dravidian movement against radical Hinduism and became a symbol of it throughout the state
